          out[((((floordiv(i.outer.outer.j.outer.outer.fused.i.outer.inner.fused.j.outer.inner.fused, 2)*65536) + (i.inner*512)) + (floormod(i.outer.outer.j.outer.outer.fused.i.outer.inner.fused.j.outer.inner.fused, 2)*256)) + j.inner)] = out.local_1[((i.inner*256) + j.inner)]
        }
      }
    }
  }
}


Execution time of this operator: max:994.163 us   median:944.385 us   min:881.673 us
